 com / eymxhrr6je loksabhaa chunaav 2019 ke duusare charan main maharashtra kii 10 loksabhaa siton par 18 april ko vot daale jaaenge
 These include Buldhana, Akola, Amravati, Hingoli, Nanded, Parbhani, Beed, Osmanabad, Latur and Solapur seats
 2014 ke lihaaj se denkhen to in 10 siton main se paanch siton par bijepi kaa kabja hai
 While Shiv Sena has three mps and two Congress mps
 is baar ke badale siyaasi sameekaran main dekhen to shivasena-bijepi or congress-ensipi gathbandhan ke bich kaante kaa muqabla mana ja rahaa he, lekin basapa or prakaash ambedkar kii party ne chunavi maidan main utarkar kai siton par trikoniya muqabla bana diya he
 Latur: From Latur Lok Sabha seat, BJP has fielded Sudhakar Tukaram Shrangare by cutting the ticket of its sitting MP Sunil Gaikwad
 jabaki congress ne kaamant machhindra, basapa ne siddharth kumaar digambararav suryavanshi or vanchit bahujan aghadi ne ram garkaar sahit 10 ummidavaar maidan main hai
 Latur seat has been the traditional seat of Shivraj Patil of Congress
 lekin bijepi is ilaake main send lagane main kaamyaab rahi thi
 Congress is betting on Kamant Machindra to bring it back
 lekin bijepi ne jis tarah se apane maujuuda saasand kaa tikat katkar shrangare ko utaara he
 With this, the BJP is facing challenges both inside and outside the party
 buldhaana:buldhaana loksabhaa seat par shivasena se jadhav prataparav ganpatrav, congress se dow rajendra bhaskaravar shingane or basapa se abdul hafeez abdul ajij sahit 12 ummidavaar maidan main hai
 The main contest is between BJP and Congress
 jadhav isse pehle do baar bijepi se saansad rah chuke hai, lekin is baar shivasena ne daanv khelaa he
 Shingne, who is contesting from Congress, has also contested from NCP twice from this seat
 haalanki unhen jeet nahin mili he
 Akola: There are 11 candidates in the Akola Lok Sabha seat, including Hidayatullah Barkatullah Patel from Congress, Dhotre Sanjay Shamrao from BJP and Prakash Ambedkar, head of the Bahujan Aghadi
 prakaash ambedkar ke siyaasi maidan main utarane se akola seat kii ladaai dilachasp ho gai he
 He has the support of Owaisi's party AIMIM
 2014 main is seat par bijepi ke dhotre ne jeet hasil kii thi
 The political struggle this time seems to be triangular
 amravati:amravati loksabhaa seat anusuchit jati ke liye arakshit he, jo shivasena kaa majboot durg mana jaataa he
 Shiv Sena has occupied this seat for the last 25 years
 shivasena ne is baar bhi apane maujuuda saansad adsul aanandarav ko utaara he
 While Navneet Kaur Rana, wife of Ravi Rana, president of the Youth Swabhiman Party, who is part of the congress-ncp alliance, has been fielded
 basapa ne arun vankhede or bahujan maha party ne athavle sanjay par daanv lagaaya he
 However, the interesting thing is that no woman has ever lost this seat, in such a situation, the alliance has relied on Navneet Kaur Rana to stop the Shiv Sena's winning streak
 hingoli:maharashtra kii hingoli seat par congress ne is baar apane maujuuda saansad rajeev saatav kii jagah shivasena se aae subhash vankhede ko utaara he
 While Shiv Sena has 17 candidates including Hemant Patil, BSP Dhanve Dutta and Altaf Ahmed from Indian Union Muslim League
 modi lahar main bhi congress is seat par jeet darj karne main kaamyaab rahi thi
 This time the Shiv Sena is hopeful of victory in the hope of splitting the Dalit and Muslim votes
 nanded:nanded loksabhaa seat congress kaa majboot garh mana jaataa he
 On the Nanded seat, Congress state president and former Chief Minister Ashok Chavan is in the fray, while BJP has fielded Chikhalikar Pratap Govindrao
 jabaki sapa ne abdul samad, vanchit bahujan aghadi ne bhinge yashpal narsingh raav, bahujan mukti party ne mohan anandarrav ko apana ummidavaar ghoshit kiya he
 Being the home area of ashok Chavan, the BJP has been deprived of feeding lotus in this area
 lekin sapa or prakaash ambedkar kii party ne is baar jis tarah se ummidavaar utaare hai
 In such a situation, the BJP is hoping to win in this area
 parabhani:parabhani loksabhaa seat shivasena kaa majboot siton main gini jaati he
 Shiv Sena has fielded its sitting MP Sanjay Haribhau Jadhav, NCP Rajesh Uttam Rao, BSP Vaijnath Sitaram and the deprived Bahujan Aghadi Alamgir Mohammad Khan
 is baar ensipi ne apane puraane ummidavaar kii jagah nae chehre par daanv lagaaya he
 While Shiv Sena is hoping for victory with its old face
 bid:maharashtra kii bid seat bijepi kaa majboot ilaaka mana jaataa he
 The BJP has fielded Pritam Munde, daughter of the late Gopinath Munde, while the NCP has fielded Bajrang Manohar Sonawane
 vanchit bahujan aghadi ne vishnu jadhav or sapa se saiyad mujammil saiyad jameel chunavi kismat aajamaa rahe hai
 Gopinath Munde won in 2014, but after his death his daughter took over the political legacy
 is baar badale siyaasi sameekaran main gopinath munde ke raajnneetik viraasat sanbhaalane kii kadi chunauti he
 But with the landing of the sp's Muslim candidate, Pritam Munde is hoping to win once again
 osmanabad:osmanabad loksabhaa seat par shivasena ne apane maujuuda saansad kaa tikat katkar omroj nimbalkar, ensipi ne ranjagit singh padmasingh patil, basapa ne shivaji pandrinath oman or vanchit bahujan aghadi kii ore se arjuna chunavi maidan main hai
 Ravindra Gaikwad won from Shiv Sena in 2014
 congress-ensipi gathbandhan kaa is seat par lambey samay tak kabja rahaa he
 In such a situation, NCP is making every effort to bring back the seat won by Shiv Sena in the Modi wave
 sholapur:sholapur loksabhaa seat congress ke diggaj netaa or purv mukhyamantri susheel kumaar scindia kaa paramparaagat kshetra rahaa he, lekin modi lahar main bijepi is ilaake main camel khilaane main kaamyaab rahi thi
 This time the Congress has fielded Sushil Kumar Shinde
 jabaki bijepi ne maujuuda saansad sharad bansode kii jagah dharmik guru jai siddheshwar shivacharya or vanchit bahujan aghadi ne ambedkar prakaash yashavanth par daanv lagaaya he
 In this seat, Lingayat and Dalit voters are in the decision making role, BJP takes advantage of Siddheshwar Shivacharya to take advantage of it, but the Congress wants to return once again with the help of Sushil Kumar Shinde

 According to the police, during the Holi on Sunday, in the spring colony of Kudipura police station, Sunil put a color on the sister of Ravi Pradhan living in the neighborhood
 rang garm pani main mila tha
 Controversy between the two sides increased
 kuch logon kii madhyasthata se vivaad haalanki samaapt ho gaya, lekin sunil ke parivaar kaa aarope he ki ravi pradhan shaam ko unke ghar aayaa or lalita (15 varsh) par kerosine daalkar aag laga di

 jila chikitsaalay main uskaa ilaaj chal rahaa he
 The police have registered a case of attempt to murder against Ravi
 kundipura ke thana prabharee jees rajput ne bataaya ki aaropee ko police ne hiraasat main le liya he
 Ram Rahim's most prominent Rajdar Honeypreet is on police remand and the biggest disclosure that Honeypreet has made to the police during the first four days of questioning is about her confidential diary
 haniprit dhire-dhire tut rahi he usne police ko apni ek aisi sikret diary ke bare main jaankaree di he, jo usne deraa main kahin chupa kar rakhi he
 According to police sources, Honeypreet has recorded not only the transaction figures but also information about many mysteries related to the dera
 sutron ke mutabik is diary main deraa sachcha sauda kii mahatvapurn baithkon kaa byora bhi darj he
 Significantly, Honeypreet is the number two in Insa Dera and was also entrusted with the responsibility of financial management of Dera Sacha Sauda
 len-dein kaa puraa kaam haniprit ke jariye hi hota tha or zyaadaatar chack bhi usee ke dwaara sin kiye jate the
 Police are making efforts to recover data from 65 computer hard disks recovered from Dera Sacha Sauda headquarters on 14 September
 police ko ab tak sirf ek hard discs se 700 karod rupye ke len-dein kii jaankaree mili he
